## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |

| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Add Evaluation Metrics Tracking

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/flipt--3d5a345f (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/flipt--3d5a345f (mirror of flipt-io/flipt)
**Your Team:** Evaluation Engine Team
**Access Scope:** You own `internal/server/evaluation/`. You may read `rpc/flipt/evaluation/` for protobuf types. Do not modify packages outside your ownership — the storage layer, HTTP/gRPC transport, authentication, and audit logging belong to other teams.

## Context

You are a developer on the Flipt Evaluation Engine team. Your team is responsible for the feature flag evaluation pipeline that determines which flag variant a user receives.

## Feature Request

**From:** Engineering Manager
**Priority:** P2
**Context:** SRE team needs visibility into evaluation throughput for capacity planning

We currently have no observability into our evaluation pipeline's throughput or error rates. When incidents occur, we can't tell whether the evaluation engine is overloaded, how many evaluations are matching vs not matching, or what our error rate looks like.

Add an in-process metrics tracker to the evaluation engine that records:
- **Total evaluations**: how many evaluations have been processed
- **Match count**: how many evaluations resulted in a successful match
- **Error count**: how many evaluations failed with errors

**YOU MUST IMPLEMENT CODE CHANGES.**

### Requirements

1. Create a new file in the evaluation package with a struct that tracks the three counters above
2. The tracker must be thread-safe — the evaluation server handles concurrent gRPC requests
3. Provide methods to record outcomes and retrieve current metric values
4. Integrate the tracker into the evaluation server so it records outcomes after each evaluation is processed
5. All changes within `internal/server/evaluation/`
6. Code compiles: `go build ./internal/server/evaluation/...`

## Success Criteria

- A metrics tracking file exists in the evaluation package
- Thread-safe implementation using appropriate synchronization
- Integrated into the evaluation server
- Go code compiles
- No changes outside `internal/server/evaluation/`

     1→package evaluation
     2→
     3→import (
     4→	"context"
     5→
     6→	"go.flipt.io/flipt/internal/storage"
     7→	"go.flipt.io/flipt/rpc/flipt"
     8→	"go.flipt.io/flipt/rpc/flipt/evaluation"
     9→	"go.uber.org/zap"
    10→	"google.golang.org/grpc"
    11→)
    12→
    13→// Storer is the minimal abstraction for interacting with the storage layer for evaluation.
    14→type Storer interface {
    15→	GetFlag(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error)
    16→	GetEvaluationRules(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRule, error)
    17→	GetEvaluationDistributions(ctx context.Context, ruleID storage.IDRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationDistribution, error)
    18→	GetEvaluationRollouts(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRollout, error)
    19→}
    20→
    21→// Server serves the Flipt evaluate v2 gRPC Server.
    22→type Server struct {
    23→	logger    *zap.Logger
    24→	store     Storer
    25→	evaluator *Evaluator
    26→	evaluation.UnimplementedEvaluationServiceServer
    27→}
    28→
    29→// New is constructs a new Server.
    30→func New(logger *zap.Logger, store Storer) *Server {
    31→	return &Server{
    32→		logger:    logger,
    33→		store:     store,
    34→		evaluator: NewEvaluator(logger, store),
    35→	}
    36→}
    37→
    38→// RegisterGRPC registers the EvaluateServer onto the provided gRPC Server.
    39→func (s *Server) RegisterGRPC(server *grpc.Server) {
    40→	evaluation.RegisterEvaluationServiceServer(server, s)
    41→}
    42→
    43→func (s *Server) AllowsNamespaceScopedAuthentication(ctx context.Context) bool {
    44→	return true
    45→}
    46→

    25→func (s *Server) Variant(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, error) {
    26→	flag, err := s.store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))
    27→	if err != nil {
    28→		return nil, err
    29→	}
    30→
    31→	s.logger.Debug("variant", zap.Stringer("request", r))
    32→
    33→	resp, err := s.variant(ctx, flag, r)
    34→	if err != nil {
    35→		return nil, err
    36→	}
    37→
    38→	spanAttrs := []attribute.KeyValue{
    39→		fliptotel.AttributeNamespace.String(r.NamespaceKey),
    40→		fliptotel.AttributeFlag.String(r.FlagKey),
    41→		fliptotel.AttributeEntityID.String(r.EntityId),
    42→		fliptotel.AttributeRequestID.String(r.RequestId),
    43→		fliptotel.AttributeMatch.Bool(resp.Match),
    44→		fliptotel.AttributeValue.String(resp.VariantKey),
    45→		fliptotel.AttributeReason.String(resp.Reason.String()),
    46→		fliptotel.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(resp.SegmentKeys),
    47→		fliptotel.AttributeFlagKey(resp.FlagKey),
    48→		fliptotel.AttributeProviderName,
    49→		fliptotel.AttributeFlagVariant(resp.VariantKey),
    50→	}
    51→
    52→	// add otel attributes to span
    53→	span := trace.SpanFromContext(ctx)
    54→	span.SetAttributes(spanAttrs...)
    55→
    56→	s.logger.Debug("variant", zap.Stringer("response", resp))
    57→	return resp, nil
    58→}

    24→// Evaluator is an evaluator for legacy flag evaluations.
    25→type Evaluator struct {
    26→	logger *zap.Logger
    27→	store  Storer
    28→}
    29→
    30→// NewEvaluator is the constructor for an Evaluator.
    31→func NewEvaluator(logger *zap.Logger, store Storer) *Evaluator {
    32→	return &Evaluator{
    33→		logger: logger,
    34→		store:  store,
    35→	}
    36→}
    37→
    38→func (e *Evaluator) Evaluate(ctx context.Context, flag *flipt.Flag, r *evaluation.EvaluationRequest) (resp *flipt.EvaluationResponse, err error) {
    39→	// Flag should be of variant type by default. However, for maximum backwards compatibility
    40→	// on this layer, we will check against the integer value of the flag type.
    41→	if int(flag.Type) != 0 || flag.Type != flipt.FlagType_VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE {
    42→		resp = &flipt.EvaluationResponse{}
    43→		resp.Reason = flipt.EvaluationReason_ERROR_EVALUATION_REASON
    44→		return resp, errs.ErrInvalidf("flag type %s invalid", flag.Type)
    45→	}
    46→
    47→	var (
    48→		startTime     = time.Now().UTC()
    49→		namespaceAttr = metrics.AttributeNamespace.String(r.NamespaceKey)
    50→		flagAttr      = metrics.AttributeFlag.String(r.FlagKey)
    51→	)

   266→// Batch takes in a list of *evaluation.EvaluationRequest and returns their respective responses.

   285→					},

     1→package evaluation
     2→
     3→import (
     4→	"sync"
     5→)
     6→
     7→// MetricsTracker tracks in-process evaluation metrics.
     8→type MetricsTracker struct {
     9→	mu          sync.RWMutex
    10→	total       int64
    11→	matchCount  int64
    12→	errorCount  int64
    13→}
    14→
    15→// NewMetricsTracker creates a new thread-safe metrics tracker.
    16→func NewMetricsTracker() *MetricsTracker {
    17→	return &MetricsTracker{}
    18→}
    19→
    20→// RecordEvaluation increments the total evaluation counter.
    21→func (m *MetricsTracker) RecordEvaluation() {
    22→	m.mu.Lock()
    23→	defer m.mu.Unlock()
    24→	m.total++
    25→}
    26→
    27→// RecordMatch increments the match count counter.
    28→func (m *MetricsTracker) RecordMatch() {
    29→	m.mu.Lock()
    30→	defer m.mu.Unlock()
    31→	m.matchCount++
    32→}
    33→
    34→// RecordError increments the error count counter.
    35→func (m *MetricsTracker) RecordError() {
    36→	m.mu.Lock()
    37→	defer m.mu.Unlock()
    38→	m.errorCount++
    39→}
    40→
    41→// GetMetrics returns a snapshot of the current metrics.
    42→func (m *MetricsTracker) GetMetrics() (total int64, matchCount int64, errorCount int64) {
    43→	m.mu.RLock()
    44→	defer m.mu.RUnlock()
    45→	return m.total, m.matchCount, m.errorCount
    46→}
    47→
    48→// Total returns the total number of evaluations.
    49→func (m *MetricsTracker) Total() int64 {
    50→	m.mu.RLock()
    51→	defer m.mu.RUnlock()
    52→	return m.total
    53→}
    54→
    55→// MatchCount returns the number of successful matches.
    56→func (m *MetricsTracker) MatchCount() int64 {
    57→	m.mu.RLock()
    58→	defer m.mu.RUnlock()
    59→	return m.matchCount
    60→}
    61→
    62→// ErrorCount returns the number of 
... (truncated)

     1→package evaluation
     2→
     3→import (
     4→	"context"
     5→
     6→	"go.flipt.io/flipt/internal/storage"
     7→	"go.flipt.io/flipt/rpc/flipt"
     8→	"go.flipt.io/flipt/rpc/flipt/evaluation"
     9→	"go.uber.org/zap"
    10→	"google.golang.org/grpc"
    11→)
    12→
    13→// Storer is the minimal abstraction for interacting with the storage layer for evaluation.
    14→type Storer interface {
    15→	GetFlag(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error)
    16→	GetEvaluationRules(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRule, error)
    17→	GetEvaluationDistributions(ctx context.Context, ruleID storage.IDRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationDistribution, error)
    18→	GetEvaluationRollouts(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRollout, error)
    19→}
    20→
    21→// Server serves the Flipt evaluate v2 gRPC Server.
    22→type Server struct {
    23→	logger          *zap.Logger
    24→	store           Storer
    25→	evaluator       *Evaluator
    26→	metricsTracker  *MetricsTracker
    27→	evaluation.UnimplementedEvaluationServiceServer
    28→}
    29→
    30→// New is constructs a new Server.
    31→func New(logger *zap.Logger, store Storer) *Server {
    32→	return &Server{
    33→		logger:         logger,
    34→		store:          store,
    35→		evaluator:      NewEvaluator(logger, store),
    36→		metricsTracker: NewMetricsTracker(),
    37→	}
    38→}
    39→
    40→// RegisterGRPC registers the EvaluateServer onto the provided gRPC Server.
    41→func (s *Server) RegisterGRPC(server *grpc.Server) {
    42→	evaluation.RegisterEvaluationServiceServer(server, s)
    43→}

Perfect! I have successfully implemented the in-process metrics tracker for the Flipt evaluation engine. Here's a summary of what was completed:

## Implementation Summary

### Files Created/Modified

**1. Created: `internal/server/evaluation/metrics_tracker.go`**
   - Thread-safe metrics tracker using `sync.RWMutex`
   - Three counters: total evaluations, match count, error count
   - Methods to record outcomes:
     - `RecordEvaluation()` - increments total evaluation counter
     - `RecordMatch()` - increments successful match counter
     - `RecordError()` - increments error counter
   - Methods to retrieve metrics:
     - `GetMetrics()` - returns snapshot of all three metrics
     - `Total()`, `MatchCount()`, `ErrorCount()` - individual getters

**2. Modified: `internal/server/evaluation/server.go`**
   - Added `metricsTracker` field to Server struct
   - Initialized tracker in `New()` constructor

**3. Modified: `internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go`**
   - Integrated tracker into `Variant()` method - tracks errors from flag lookup
   - Integrated tracker into `Boolean()` method - tracks errors from flag lookup and type validation
   - Integrated tracker into `variant()` internal method - records evaluations, matches, and errors
   - Integrated tracker into `boolean()` internal method - records evaluations, matches (when reason is MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON), and errors
   - Integrated tracker into `Batch()` method - tracks errors for NOT_FOUND cases

**4. Created: `internal/server/evaluation/metrics_tracker_test.go`**
   - Comprehensive unit tests for the metrics tracker
   - Tests for individual operations
   - Concurrent/thread-safety tests

### Key Features

✅ **Thread-Safe**: Uses `sync.RWMutex` for safe concurrent access by gRPC handlers

1. WRITE /workspace/internal/server/evaluation/metrics_tracker.go
package evaluation

import (
	"sync"
)

// MetricsTracker tracks in-process evaluation metrics.
type MetricsTracker struct {
	mu          sync.RWMutex
	total       int64
	matchCount  int64
	errorCount  int64
}

// NewMetricsTracker creates a new thread-safe metrics tracker.
func NewMetricsTracker() *MetricsTracker {
	return &MetricsTracker{}
}

// RecordEvaluation increments the total evaluation counter.
func (m *MetricsTracker) RecordEvaluation() {
	m.mu.Lock()
	defer m.mu.Unlock()
	m.total++
}

// RecordMatch increments the match count counter.
func (m *MetricsTracker) RecordMatch() {
	m.mu.Lock()
	defer m.mu.Unlock()
	m.matchCount++
}

// RecordError increments the error count counter.
func (m *MetricsTracker) RecordError() {
	m.mu.Lock()
	defer m.mu.Unlock()
	m.errorCount++
}

// GetMetrics returns a snapshot of the current metrics.
func (m *MetricsTracker) GetMetrics() (total int64, matchCount int64, errorCount int64) {
	m.mu.RLock()
	defer m.mu.RUnlock()
	return m.total, m.matchCount, m.errorCount
}

// Total returns the total number of evaluations.
func (m *MetricsTracker) Total() int64 {
	m.mu.RLock()
	defer m.mu.RUnlock()
	return m.total
}

// MatchCount returns the number of successful matches.
func (m *MetricsTracker) MatchCount() int64 {
	m.mu.RLock()
	defer m.mu.RUnlock()
	return m.matchCount
}

// ErrorCount returns the number of evaluation errors.
func (m *MetricsTracker) ErrorCount() int64 {
	m.mu.RLock()
	defer m.mu.RUnlock()
	return m.errorCount
}

5. EDIT /workspace/internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go
Before
func (s *Server) variant(ctx context.Context, flag *flipt.Flag, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, error) {
	resp, err := s.evaluator.Evaluate(ctx, flag, r)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	var reason rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason

	switch resp.Reason {
	case flipt.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON:
		reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON
	case flipt.EvaluationReason_FLAG_DISABLED_EVALUATION_REASON:
		reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_FLAG_DISABLED_EVALUATION_REASON
	default:
		reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_UNKNOWN_EVALUATION_REASON
	}

	ver := &rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse{
		RequestId:         r.RequestId,
		Match:             resp.Match,
		Reason:            reason,
		VariantKey:        resp.Value,
		VariantAttachment: resp.Attachment,
		FlagKey:           resp.FlagKey,
	}

	if len(resp.SegmentKeys) > 0 {
		ver.SegmentKeys = resp.SegmentKeys
	}

	return ver, nil
}
After
func (s *Server) variant(ctx context.Context, flag *flipt.Flag, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, error) {
	s.metricsTracker.RecordEvaluation()

	resp, err := s.evaluator.Evaluate(ctx, flag, r)
	if err != nil {
		s.metricsTracker.RecordError()
		return nil, err
	}

	var reason rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason

	switch resp.Reason {
	case flipt.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON:
		reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON
	case flipt.EvaluationReason_FLAG_DISABLED_EVALUATION_REASON:
		reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_FLAG_DISABLED_EVALUATION_REASON
	default:
		reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_UNKNOWN_EVALUATION_REASON
	}

	ver := &rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse{
		RequestId:         r.RequestId,
		Match:             resp.Match,
		Reason:            reason,
		VariantKey:        resp.Value,
		VariantAttachment: resp.Attachment,
		FlagKey:           resp.FlagKey,
	}

	if len(resp.SegmentKeys) > 0 {
		ver.SegmentKeys = resp.SegmentKeys
	}

	if resp.Match {
		s.metricsTracker.RecordMatch()
	}

	return ver, nil
}

// Boolean evaluates a request for a boolean flag and entity.
func (s *Server) Boolean(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BooleanEvaluationResponse, error) {
	flag, err := s.store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))

		s.metricsTracker.RecordEvaluation()

		s.metricsTracker.RecordError()

9. WRITE /workspace/internal/server/evaluation/metrics_tracker_test.go
package evaluation

import (
	"testing"

	"github.com/stretchr/testify/assert"
)

func TestMetricsTracker_RecordEvaluation(t *testing.T) {
	tracker := NewMetricsTracker()

	total, matches, errors := tracker.GetMetrics()
	assert.Equal(t, int64(0), total)
	assert.Equal(t, int64(0), matches)
	assert.Equal(t, int64(0), errors)

	tracker.RecordEvaluation()
	total, matches, errors = tracker.GetMetrics()
	assert.Equal(t, int64(1), total)
	assert.Equal(t, int64(0), matches)
	assert.Equal(t, int64(0), errors)

	tracker.RecordEvaluation()
	total, matches, errors = tracker.GetMetrics()
	assert.Equal(t, int64(2), total)
	assert.Equal(t, int64(0), matches)
	assert.Equal(t, int64(0), errors)
}

func TestMetricsTracker_RecordMatch(t *testing.T) {
	tracker := NewMetricsTracker()

	tracker.RecordEvaluation()
	tracker.RecordMatch()

	total, matches, errors := tracker.GetMetrics()
	assert.Equal(t, int64(1), total)
	assert.Equal(t, int64(1), matches)
	assert.Equal(t, int64(0), errors)
}

func TestMetricsTracker_RecordError(t *testing.T) {
	tracker := NewMetricsTracker()

	tracker.RecordEvaluation()
	tracker.RecordError()

	total, matches, errors := tracker.GetMetrics()
	assert.Equal(t, int64(1), total)
	assert.Equal(t, int64(0), matches)
	assert.Equal(t, int64(1), errors)
}

	tracker.RecordMatch()

	tracker.RecordEvaluation()
	tracker.RecordError()

	tracker.RecordEvaluation()
	tracker.RecordError()

	tracker.RecordEvaluation()

	total, matches, errors := tracker.GetMetrics()
	assert.Equal(t, int64(5), total)
	assert.Equal(t, int64(2), matches)

10. EDIT /workspace/internal/server/evaluation/metrics_tracker_test.go
Before
func TestMetricsTracker_ThreadSafe(t *testing.T) {
	tracker := NewMetricsTracker()

	// Test concurrent writes
	done := make(chan bool, 10)

	for i := 0; i < 10; i++ {
		go func() {
			tracker.RecordEvaluation()
			if i%2 == 0 {
				tracker.RecordMatch()
			}
			done <- true
		}()
	}

	for i := 0; i < 10; i++ {
		<-done
	}

	total := tracker.Total()
	matches := tracker.MatchCount()
	assert.Equal(t, int64(10), total)
	assert.Equal(t, int64(5), matches)
}
After
func TestMetricsTracker_ThreadSafe(t *testing.T) {
	tracker := NewMetricsTracker()

	// Test concurrent writes
	done := make(chan bool, 10)

	for i := 0; i < 10; i++ {
		go func(idx int) {
			tracker.RecordEvaluation()
			if idx%2 == 0 {
				tracker.RecordMatch()
			}
			done <- true
		}(i)
	}

	for i := 0; i < 10; i++ {
		<-done
	}

	total := tracker.Total()
	matches := tracker.MatchCount()
	assert.Equal(t, int64(10), total)
	assert.Equal(t, int64(5), matches)
}
